ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">Media caption, </span><div spacing="6" class="ssrcss-y7krbn-Stack e1y4nx260"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Video shows people running to escape Russian shelling in Irpin, just outside of the capital Kyiv</p></div></figcaption></figure></div><div data-component="text-block" class="ssrcss-uf6wea-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0"><div class="ssrcss-7uxr49-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">President Volodymyr Zelensky has said everyone who commits atrocities against Ukraine&#x27;s civilians will be punished.</b></p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">He said Ukrainians would not forgive or forget, and accused invading Russian troops of deliberate murder.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">&quot;There will be no quiet place on Earth for you. Except for the grave,&quot; the president said.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Ukrainian officials say Russia is striking civilian targets around the country, including hospitals, nurseries, and schools.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">But Russia denies targeting civilians, saying it is carrying out a &quot;special military operation&quot; against Ukrainian &quot;nationalists&quot; and &quot;neo-Nazis&quot;.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Ukraine&#x27;s Deputy Prime Minister Olha Stefanishyna told the BBC that, after &quot;strong resistance&quot; from the Ukrainian army, there was an &quot;enormous operation&quot; by Russia against civilians.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">On Sunday alone, a family of four were killed when Russian forces fired shells at people fleeing the conflict in the town of Irpin, north-west of Kyiv.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">And in the port city of Mariupol, promised evacuations were cancelled on both Saturday and Sunday amid fresh attacks.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The city council there said Russian shelling had made safe movement impossible. Russia has blamed Ukrainian forces.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The city is now in its sixth day with no running water, no power, and no sanitation. Food and water are fast running out.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Moscow announced it would open new evacuation corridors at 09:00 local time (07:00 GMT) in Mariupol and other cities. However, the routes published by Russia&#x27;s RIA Novosti news agency show some of the corridors end in Russia and Belarus.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The corridor from Kyiv will lead to Russian ally Belarus, and civilians from Kharkiv will only have a corridor leading to Russia.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Corridors from the cities of Mariupol and Sumy will lead both to other Ukrainian cities and to Russia, the AFP news agency reports.</p></div></div><div data-component="image-block" class="ssrcss-1b5y2ub-ComponentWrapper-FullWidthWrapper morning</p></div></figcaption></figure></div><div data-component="text-block" class="ssrcss-uf6wea-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0"><div class="ssrcss-7uxr49-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p judgment.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">&quot;We will not forgive, we will not forget, we will punish everyone who committed atrocities in this war on our land,&quot; he said. e1jhz7w10">&quot;Thousands of people work there. Hundreds of thousands live nearby. This is murder. Premeditated murder,&quot; he said.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">He also condemned Western governments for failing to speak out against the plan.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The World Health Organization said health facilities were being attacked, with its director-general Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus <a href="https://twitter.com/DrTedros/status/1500372569425387522" class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0">saying they had caused &quot;multiple deaths and injuries&quot;.<span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a></p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The British government has accused Russia of targeting populated areas &quot;in multiple locations&quot;, noting in an <a href="https://twitter.com/DefenceHQ/status/1500357239428763649/photo/1" class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0">intelligence update<span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a> that it had &quot;previously used similar tactics in Chechnya in 1999 and Syria in 2016&quot;. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">On Sunday, UN monitors said 364 civilian deaths had been confirmed in Ukraine since the invasion began on 24 February, but the real figure was likely to be &quot;considerably higher&quot;. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The UNHCR said more than 1.5 million people had fled Ukraine since Russia invaded.</p></div></div><div e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Attacking civilians and civilian infrastructure - such as schools and hospitals - is against the <a href="https://www.icrc.org/en/war-and-law/treaties-customary-law/geneva-conventions" class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0">Geneva Conventions,<span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a> which are treaties agreed by all countries that are supposed to regulate war.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">As well as the WHO, other non-government organisations have also reported attacks on civilian targets.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Amnesty International <a href="https://twitter.com/amnesty/status/1498710993391828994" class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0">says it has verified various attacks<span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a> - including cluster munitions hitting a kindergarten and nursery, and a ballistic missile hitting a hospital.</p></div></div><div data-component="image-block"
